module MenhirBasics = struct
  
  exception Error
  
  let _eRR =
    fun _s ->
      raise Error
  
  type token = 
    | WITH
    | UNIT_T
    | UNDERSCORE
    | TYPE
    | TRUE
    | TIMES
    | TILDE_ARROW
    | THEN
    | STRING_T
    | STRING of (
# 3 "lib/parsing/parser.mly"
       (string)
# 24 "lib/parsing/parser.ml"
  )
    | SND
    | SEMICOLON
    | RPAREN
    | RIGHT
    | RBRACKET
    | PLUS
    | OR
    | NOT
    | NEQ
    | MINUS
    | MATCH
    | LT
    | LPAREN
    | LET
    | LEQ
    | LEFT
    | LBRACKET
    | INT_T
    | INT of (
# 2 "lib/parsing/parser.mly"
       (int)
# 47 "lib/parsing/parser.ml"
  )
    | IN
    | IF
    | ID of (
# 1 "lib/parsing/parser.mly"
       (string)
# 54 "lib/parsing/parser.ml"
  )
    | GT
    | GEQ
    | FUN
    | FST
    | FOREIGN
    | FALSE
    | EQ
    | EOF
    | ELSE
    | DOT
    | DIV
    | COMMA
    | COLONEQ
    | COLON
    | BOOL_T
    | BAR
    | ARROW
    | AND
  
end

include MenhirBasics

# 39 "lib/parsing/parser.mly"
  
  open Ast_core.Local.M
  open Ast_core.Choreo.M
  open Parsed_ast

  let gen_pos startpos endpos =
    let open Lexing in
    { Pos_info.fname = startpos.pos_fname
    ; start = startpos.pos_lnum, startpos.pos_cnum - startpos.pos_bol
    ; stop = endpos.pos_lnum, endpos.pos_cnum - endpos.pos_bol
    }

# 92 "lib/parsing/parser.ml"

type ('s, 'r) _menhir_state = 
  | MenhirState000 : ('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 000.
        Stack shape : .
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState005 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_TYPE _menhir_cell0_typ_id, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 005.
        Stack shape : TYPE typ_id.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState007 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_LPAREN, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 007.
        Stack shape : LPAREN.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState010 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_loc_id, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 010.
        Stack shape : loc_id.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState013 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_LPAREN, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 013.
        Stack shape : LPAREN.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState017 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_local_type _menhir_cell0_TIMES, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 017.
        Stack shape : local_type TIMES.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState020 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_local_type _menhir_cell0_PLUS, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 020.
        Stack shape : local_type PLUS.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState024 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_choreo_type _menhir_cell0_TIMES, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 024.
        Stack shape : choreo_type TIMES.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState027 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_choreo_type _menhir_cell0_PLUS, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state
    (** State 027.
        Stack shape : choreo_type PLUS.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState029 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_choreo_type, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state

        Stack shape : choreo_type.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState034 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_RIGHT, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state

        Stack shape : RIGHT.
        Start symbol: prog. *)

  | MenhirState035 : (('s, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_cell1_LPAREN, _menhir_box_prog) _menhir_state

let _menhir_print_token : token -> string =
  fun _tok ->
    match _tok with
    | AND ->
        "AND"
    | ARROW ->
        "ARROW"
    | BAR ->
        "BAR"
    | BOOL_T ->
        "BOOL_T"
    | COLON ->
        "COLON"
    | COLONEQ ->
        "COLONEQ"
    | COMMA ->
        "COMMA"
    | DIV ->
        "DIV"
    | DOT ->
        "DOT"
    | ELSE ->
        "ELSE"
    | EOF ->
        "EOF"
    | EQ ->
        "EQ"
    | FALSE ->
        "FALSE"
    | FOREIGN ->
        "FOREIGN"
    | FST ->
        "FST"
    | FUN ->
        "FUN"
    | GEQ ->
        "GEQ"
    | GT ->
        "GT"
    | ID _ ->
        "ID"
    | IF ->
        "IF"
    | IN ->
        "IN"
    | INT _ ->
        "INT"
    | INT_T ->
        "INT_T"
    | LBRACKET ->
        "LBRACKET"
    | LEFT ->
        "LEFT"
    | LEQ ->
        "LEQ"
    | LET ->
        "LET"
    | LPAREN ->
        "LPAREN"
    | LT ->
        "LT"
    | MATCH ->
        "MATCH"
    | MINUS ->
        "MINUS"
    | NEQ ->
        "NEQ"
    | NOT ->
        "NOT"
    | OR ->
        "OR"
    | PLUS ->
        "PLUS"
    | RBRACKET ->
        "RBRACKET"
    | RIGHT ->
        "RIGHT"
    | RPAREN ->
        "RPAREN"
    | SEMICOLON ->
        "SEMICOLON"
    | SND ->
        "SND"
    | STRING _ ->
        "STRING"
    | STRING_T ->
        "STRING_T"
    | THEN ->
        "THEN"
    | TILDE_ARROW ->
        "TILDE_ARROW"
    | TIMES ->
        "TIMES"
    | TRUE ->
        "TRUE"
    | TYPE ->
        "TYPE"
    | UNDERSCORE ->
        "UNDERSCORE"
    | UNIT_T ->
        "UNIT_T"
    | WITH ->
        "WITH"

let _menhir_fail : unit -> 'a =
  fun () ->
    Printf.eprintf "Internal failure -- please contact the parser generator's developers.\n%!";
    assert false
